<script>
        function getScrollbarWidth() {
            const scrollDiv = document.createElement('div')
            scrollDiv.style = 'position: absolute;top: -9999px;width: 50px;height: 50px;overflow: scroll;'
            document.body.appendChild(scrollDiv)
            const scrollbarWidth = scrollDiv.getBoundingClientRect().width - scrollDiv.clientWidth
            document.body.removeChild(scrollDiv)
            return scrollbarWidth
        }

        function header() {
            return {
                hasScrolled: false,
                compact: false,
                menuOpen: false,
                subMenuOpen: false,
                submenuOpenedId: '',
                isMobile: false,
                searchOpen: false,
                searchHasFocus: false,
                searchTerm: '',
                searchInput: null,
                hiddenSearchInput: null,
                scrollWidth: 0,
                handleToggleMenu() {
                    this.compact = false
                    this.searchOpen = false
                    this.scrollWidth = getScrollbarWidth()
                    if (!this.menuOpen) {
                        document.body.style.paddingRight = `${this.scrollWidth}px`
                        this.$refs.fixedHeader.style.paddingRight = `${this.scrollWidth}px`
                        this.$refs.fixedMenu.style.paddingRight = `${this.scrollWidth}px`
                    } else {
                        this.$refs.fixedHeader.style.paddingRight = null
                        this.$refs.fixedMenu.style.paddingRight = null
                        document.body.style.paddingRight = null
                    }
                    this.menuOpen = !this.menuOpen
                    this.menuOpen ? document.body.classList.add('overflow-hidden') : document.body.classList.remove(
                        'overflow-hidden')
                },
                checkScroll() {
                    if (window.scrollY > 56) {
                        this.hasScrolled = true
                    } else {
                        this.hasScrolled = false
                    }
                },
                handleToggleSubmenu(id) {
                    if (!this.isMobile) return
                    this.submenuOpenedId = !this.subMenuOpen ? id.toString() : '';
                    this.subMenuOpen = !this.subMenuOpen;
                },
                checkMobile() {
                    const widthOfScreen = 1024
                    this.isMobile = window.innerWidth < widthOfScreen;
                    if (!this.isMobile) {
                        this.submenuOpenedId = '';
                        this.subMenuOpen = false;
                    }
                },
                openSearch($dispatch) {
                    this.menuOpen = false
                    this.compact = true
                    $dispatch('search-open')
                    this.searchOpen = true
                    this.subMenuOpen = false
                    document.body.classList.add('h-screen', 'overflow-hidden')
                    this.$nextTick(() => {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            this.$refs.searchInput.focus()
                        }, 50)
                    })
                    if (localStorage.hasOwnProperty('locker.lastSearch')) {
                        this.searchTerm = localStorage.getItem('locker.lastSearch');
                    }
                },
                closeSearch($dispatch) {
                    this.compact = false
                    $dispatch('search-closed')
                    this.searchOpen = false
                    this.searchHasFocus = false
                    // this.searchTerm = null
                    document.body.classList.remove('h-screen', 'overflow-hidden')
                },
                clearSearch() {
                    this.searchHasFocus = true
                    this.searchTerm = '';
                    this.$nextTick(() => {
                        this.$refs.searchInput.focus()
                    })
                },
                focusSearch(state) {
                    this.searchHasFocus = state
                },
                cartAddOrderCode(orderCode) {
                    Livewire.emit('events.cart.add.order_code', orderCode)
                }
            }
        }

    </script>
</header>

<div class="container relative">
<h1 class="text-4xl sm:text-5xl font-medium leading-none mb-2">
    Privacy Statement
</h1>
<div class="h-8"></div>
</div>
<div class="prose prose-sm container space-y-6">
<p>This statement applies to Balluff, Inc. and the <a href="http://www.balluff.us/" target="_blank">www.balluff.us</a> web site.</p><p>Balluff Inc., a wholly owned subsidiary of Balluff GmbH, is sensitive to privacy issues on the Internet. We believe it is important you know how we treat the information about you we receive on the Internet. This statement describes our Standard Privacy Policy with respect to:</p><ul><li><p>What Information is Collected; How Information is Collected; and by Whom is Information Collected</p></li><li><p>The Sharing of Collected Information</p></li><li><p>How You Can Access, Change or Limit the Information Collected About You</p></li><li><p>Security of Information</p></li></ul><p><strong>What Information is Collected; How Information is Collected; and by Whom is Information Collected</strong></p><p>In general, you can visit Balluff Inc. on the World Wide Web without telling us who you are or revealing any information about yourself. Our web servers collect the domain names, not the email addresses, of visitors. This information is aggregated to measure the number of visits, average time spent on the site, pages viewed, etc. BALLUFF Inc. uses this information to measure the use of our site and to improve the content of our site.</p><p>There are times, however, when we may need information from you, such as your name and address. When information is needed, we will try to let you know at the time of collection, how we will use the personal information. This personally identifiable information will never knowingly appear in public areas of our Web site. The personal information we collect is used only by us to respond to your inquiry, process a literature order or allow you to access specific account information or premium content.</p><p>In addition, we aggregate the general information and the personal information. We compile and analyze this aggregated information so that we can provide more meaningful information to corporate partners and more relevant content and advertisements to you.</p><p>You remain in control of your information. Balluff Inc. will NOT use or share the personal information we collect in ways unrelated to the purpose for which you provided the information without first obtaining your consent (opt-in). At the time you provide your information, you can choose whether you want to receive further communications about special offers, product information or other marketing messages. If you do opt-in to marketing communications from Balluff, Inc., you can opt-out at any time. All email communications from us, such as newsletters, tell you how to stop receiving them.</p><p><strong>The Sharing of Collected Information</strong></p><p>Occasionally, we may make the email addresses, of those who provide this information, available to other reputable organizations whose products or services we think you may find interesting. In these cases, you will be offered an opportunity to limit access to your information.</p><p>If you register with a BALLUFF Inc. business partner online, we may use this information to provide you with custom information about BALLUFF Inc.'s offering in support of your business needs. A technology called cookies may be used to provide you with tailored information. A cookie is a tiny element of data that a web site can send to your browser, which may then be stored on your hard drive so we can recognize you when you return. You may set your browser to notify you when you receive a cookie.</p><p>At times we conduct online surveys to better understand the needs and profile of our visitors. When we conduct a survey, we will try to let you know how we will use the information at the time we collect information from you on the Internet.</p><p>BALLUFF Inc.'s website may contain links to other sites such as other Balluff locations worldwide or BALLUFF Inc. distributors and sales affiliates. While we try to link only to sites that share our high standards and respect for privacy, we are not responsible for the content or the privacy practices employed by other sites.</p><p><strong>How You Can Access, Change or Limit the Information Collected About You</strong></p><p>You can request that the information collected about you be updated at any time by sending an email request to <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0d6f6c6161786b6b4d6f6c6161786b6b236e6260"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="6e2c0f02021b08082e0c0f02021b0808400d0103">[email protected]</span></a> or call 1-800-543-8390.</p><p><strong>Security</strong></p><p>Balluff Inc. uses the highest security standard available (SSL) to encrypt all of your account, credit card and personally identifiable information while it is in transit to us. All data stored on the Balluff Inc. server is protected by a secure "firewall" so that no unauthorized use or activity can take place. Although Balluff Inc. will make every effort to safeguard your personal information from loss, misuse or alteration by third parties, you should be aware that there is always some risk that thieves may find a way to thwart our security system or that transmissions over the Internet will be intercepted.</p>
</div>

<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
        function countryList() {
            return {
                selected: null,
                openRegion(region) {
                    if(this.selected !== region) {
                        this.selected = region
                        const newPosition  = (region -1)  * this.$refs['region'+region].previousElementSibling.offsetHeight
                        const currentPosition = this.$refs.list.scrollTop

                        if(currentPosition < newPosition ) {
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                this.$refs.list.scrollTo({top: newPosition, behavior: 'smooth'})
                            }, 300);
                        }
                        else {
                            this.$refs.list.scrollTo({top: newPosition, behavior: 'smooth'})
                        }
                    } else {
                        this.selected = null
                        this.$refs.list.scrollTo({top: 0, behavior: 'smooth'})
                    }
                },
            }
        }
    </script>

         loading: false,

         fullPageLoadingBlacklist: [
            {
                component: 'balluff-one.cart.widget',

            }, {

                component: 'webshop.product.variant-selector',

            }, {

                methods: ['toggleFilterOpen', '$set-showColumnPicker']
            }, {
                component: 'webshop.product.change-configuration-button',
                methods: ['$set-showDialog']
            }
        ],
        isOnBlacklist: function(component, methods = null) {
            const blacklistedComponent = this.fullPageLoadingBlacklist.find((item) =&gt; item.component === component)
            // console.log(methods)
            if (! blacklistedComponent) {
                 return false
            }

            if (!blacklistedComponent.methods) {
                 return true;
            }

            return !! blacklistedComponent.methods.filter(item =&gt; methods.includes(item)).length
        },
        composeStackName: function(component, methods) {
            return component + '-'  + methods.join('-')
        },
        getMethodsTriggered: function(message) {
            // console.log(message)
            return message.updateQueue.map(item =&gt; {
                // We catch methods, params (for wire model separated with -), prop names, events
                const method = item.method === '$set' ? '$set-' + item?.payload?.params[0] : item.method
                return method || item.name || item.payload.event
            })
        }
     }" x-init="
        Livewire.hook('message.sent', (message, component) =&gt; {
            const componentName = component.fingerprint.name
            const methodsTriggered = getMethodsTriggered(message)

            if (isOnBlacklist(componentName, methodsTriggered)) {
                 return
            }

            loadingStack.push(composeStackName(componentName, methodsTriggered))

            loading = true
        } );

        Livewire.hook('message.processed', (message, component) =&gt; {
            const componentName = component.fingerprint.name
            const methodsTriggered = getMethodsTriggered(message)

            if (isOnBlacklist(componentName, methodsTriggered)) {
                 return
            }

            loadingStack = loadingStack.filter(item =&gt; item !== composeStackName(componentName, methodsTriggered))

            if (!loadingStack.length) {
               loading = false
            }
        });

            container: $refs.bodymovin,
            renderer: 'svg',
            loop: true,
            autoplay: true,

        });
